DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `committee_members`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `committee_members` (
  `no` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `member` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `committee` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`no`),
  KEY `committee_members_member_foreign` (`member`),
  KEY `committee_members_committee_foreign` (`committee`),
  CONSTRAINT `committee_members_committee_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`committee`) REFERENCES `committees` (`no`),
  CONSTRAINT `committee_members_member_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`member`) REFERENCES `users` (`no`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=9 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

--
-- Table structure for table `contents_evaluations`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `contents_evaluations`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `contents_evaluations` (
  `no` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `content` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `student` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `score` int(11) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`no`),
  KEY `contents_evaluations_content_foreign` (`content`),
  KEY `contents_evaluations_student_foreign` (`student`),
  CONSTRAINT `contents_evaluations_content_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`content`) REFERENCES `contents` (`no`),
  CONSTRAINT `contents_evaluations_student_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`student`) REFERENCES `users` (`no`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

/*!40000 ALTER TABLE `contents_evaluations` ENABLE KEYS */;

-- Table structure for table `contents_package_shares`

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `contents_package_shares`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `contents_package_shares` (
  `no` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `contents_package` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `img_url` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `explain` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `views` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `downloads` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '이름',
  PRIMARY KEY (`no`),
  KEY `contents_package_shares_contents_package_foreign` (`contents_package`),
  CONSTRAINT `contents_package_shares_contents_package_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`contents_package`) REFERENCES `contents_packages` (`no`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=32 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;
